Recent Bandit Situation in Hunan Province 52

Changsha Correspondence: The Hunan Rehabilitation Committee held an emergency meeting on the 6th of this month, as the banditry has been spreading, and relying solely on a portion of the Fourth Route Army is not sufficient to suppress them. It was decided to appoint Huang Zhenyuan as a representative to go to Nanjing to petition the National Government and the Fourth Plenary Session to dispatch a large army to encircle and suppress the communist bandits in the three provinces. Simultaneously, telegrams were sent to public organizations in Hubei and Jiangxi provinces, requesting them to send representatives to the capital to petition as well. Peng Zhaohuang was also appointed as a representative to visit He Jian, requesting attention to blocking and intercepting the bandits to prevent the provincial capital from suffering from bandit disasters again. The bandit situation in various areas is described as follows: In the Jinli area, after the bandits led by He Kuang and others captured Nanhua, He Jian dispatched the 16th Division Commander Peng Weiren, leading the Liu Jiren and Cheng Tiexia brigades, from Yuanjiang to suppress the bandits in western Hunan. The bandit suppression commander Dai Huiyuan, leading the Li Guojun and Xiang Kequan groups, advanced from Hanshou and Yuanjiang to suppress them. The Sichuan Army under Lai Xinhui, Zhang Ying and Ma Kunshan's divisions, advanced from Anxiang to suppress them. The First Garrison Commander Chen Quzhen's forces, Chen Yunkui and Dai Jitao's groups, advanced from Jinshi and Lizhou to suppress them in all directions. Consequently, on the 30th of last month, Nanhua County was recaptured. On the 1st of this month, Meitian Lake was recaptured, and on the 3rd, Huarong was recaptured. Initially, it was thought that the bandits had fled back to Hubei Province, but unexpectedly, He Kuang and others adopted a feint to the east and attacked Jinshi from the Lianyu Xu by surprise. As only Chen Yunkui and Dai Jitao's groups were stationed there, they could not resist due to the disparity in numbers and were forced to retreat and defend Lizhou County. Jinshi was lost on the 4th. That night, the bandits pursued and besieged Lizhou, launching a fierce attack. On the 5th, Lizhou also fell. Chen and Dai's troops retreated to defend He Kou. The Lizhou County Magistrate Zuo Zonggu fled to Linli. He Jian was extremely anxious upon receiving the news and immediately sent telegrams to Peng Weiren and the Sichuan Army's Zhang and Ma divisions, ordering them to advance from Anxiang towards Jinshi and Lizhou. He ordered Dai Huiyuan and Li Guojun to lead their troops to encircle and attack Jinshi and Lizhou from Changde and Linli. Chen Quzhen was ordered to lead his troops to block the area of Shimen He Kou to prevent them from advancing further. He also ordered the Changtao Garrison Commander He Ying to be on alert in Changde and Taoyuan. It is reported that after He Kuang and others captured Jinshi and Lizhou, they threatened to invade Changde and Taoyuan. In the Cha An area, the most urgent bandit situation in Hunan Province is in the Chaling Youxian Anren area in eastern Hunan, in addition to Jinli in western Hunan. A part of the communist bandits under Zhu Mao, after entering Hunan from Lianhua in western Jiangxi, joined Chen Shao's gang and captured Chaling on the 2nd of this month, and Anren on the 6th. The defending forces there were the 19th Division's Deng Nanji Brigade and the Liling Guard Corps' Yu Gongqian's forces, who have now retreated to defend Youxian. Upon receiving the news, He Jian telegraphed the Hunan Southern Garrison Commander Duan Heng and the Hunan Southern Militia First Column Commander Zeng Zhengyan to quickly defend the Lai Shui and Xiang Shui lines to strictly prevent them from advancing. He also telegraphed the 19th Division Commander Li Jue, ordering him to lead the troops stationed in Pingxiang back to Hunan to attack in Youxian and Liling. Currently, the people in various counties in eastern Hunan have fled to Changsha and Hengzhou to seek refuge. In the Pingliu area, Pingjiang and Liuyang counties have long been bandit dens. The pseudo-Red Army Red Guards (i.e., bandits with spears) in Liuyang claim to have as many as six divisions, and even more in Pingjiang. The armed bandits in Pingjiang and Liuyang were originally the gangs of Kong Hechong and Li Shixing, with three to four thousand guns. Recently, Huang Gonglue has fled from Jiangxi into Pingjiang, and Peng Dehuai's main force will also flee back to the old nests of Pingjiang and Liuyang, leading to an extremely tense situation. The 30th Division Commander Tao Guang is currently defending the Zhusha Ao and Genggu Tai area on the Changping border. Since the 3rd, the communist bandits have again attacked Zhusha Ao and Genggu Tai. After four days and nights of fierce fighting, Tao Guang supervised the Hou Pengfei, Zhong Guangren, and Chen Wo brigades, as well as the Second Bandit Suppression Battalion led by Zhu Xingshu, to launch a counterattack. Although many were killed or captured, the bandits have not yet retreated and are still in a stalemate. In the Liuyang area, Chen Guangzhong and Bai Shinou's forces are currently stationed near the county seat, preparing to first eliminate the scattered bandits in the vicinity and then suppress them in the surrounding villages. (November 7th)

Petition in Nanjing by People from Hubei and Jiangxi Provinces 53

Hankou Correspondence: Since the communist bandits captured Ji'an on the 5th of last month, more than eight divisions have been sent to aid Jiangxi, but Ji'an has not yet been recovered. The people from Jiangxi in Wuhan have specially appointed representatives Liu Shaoqing, Yang Zhensheng, and more than ten others to take the Fengyang Maru to Nanjing on the evening of the 9th to petition for the swift suppression of the communist bandits in Ji'an and to request funds for disaster relief. It is reported that if this trip does not yield satisfactory results, they will appeal to the Fourth Plenary Session to achieve their goals. The petition presented by the representatives in Nanjing is as follows: Firstly, we urgently request the military and political authorities of Jiangxi Province to swiftly dispatch a strong army to jointly suppress the communist bandits in Ji'an to save the people and maintain the overall situation. Unfortunately, Jiangxi is plagued by communist bandits, and the ten counties under the jurisdiction of Ji'an, an old prefecture in western Jiangxi, have long been reduced to red areas, where they search and burn deeds, excavate fields, gather in the villages, and demand everything from every household, using every means. The good people have nowhere to stand and can only take refuge in Ji'an. This time, the Zhu Mao communist bandits led a large force of bandits, crossed into Lianhua from Xiang, and suddenly raided Ji'an County on the 5th of last month. The county was lost, the red flames soared into the sky, and the cries shook the wilderness. The refugees who fled from Ji'an had no way to survive and could not even seek death. It was truly an unprecedented catastrophe. According to the emergency reports from the Ji'an refugees, the bandits are killing hundreds of people every day. Those with a little property are kidnapped and extorted, and young women are imprisoned and raped. The stores and households are looted clean. In severe cases, farmers are ordered to take revenge and kill each household, resulting in piles of corpses and rivers of blood. This tragic scene is heartbreaking. The Ji'an refugees have repeatedly telegraphed the provincial authorities, urging them to quickly send troops to advance and suppress the bandits, but for more than a month, there has been no sign of advance. We do not understand why. Currently, the communist bandits entrenched in Ji'an are actively organizing a Soviet government, establishing a Communist Party headquarters, and implementing communist work. If we allow this to continue to spread, not only will millions of lives be lost, but the situation in the provincial capital will also be in danger. Even more tragically, the ten counties of Ji'an have been looted clean. Even if we recover them, the remaining refugees will have no clothes or food and will either die from gunfire or starvation. Therefore, we rushed to Nanjing day and night to petition your government to quickly telegraph Chairman Lu to swiftly dispatch a capable army to Ji'an to suppress the bandits in the ten counties, and to telegraph Chief Commander Liu to return to Jiangxi to cooperate in suppressing the bandits, with a deadline to recover Ji'an and the ten counties under its jurisdiction. We also ask for funds to be allocated for disaster relief to save the people from fire and water and to stabilize the overall situation. With tears in our eyes, we present this urgent plea and await your orders.

Overseas Chinese in Nanyang Appeal for the Xu Case 54

The Xu Zhuoran assassination case in Xiamen has now been transferred to the Hangzhou District Court for trial. The people of Fujian are paying close attention to this, and the overseas Chinese in Nanyang are particularly concerned. Recently, the Tong'an Fellow Association of the Fujianese in Batavia, Java, in Nanyang, sent another telegram to the Judicial Yuan and the Higher and Local Courts of Hangzhou, stating that Xu Zhuoran was a pillar of the party and the nation, and his assassination caused great sorrow among the people. Since the occurrence of this case, all eyes have been on it, hoping that the perpetrators would be apprehended and punished according to the law. Unexpectedly, Mr. Chen Yanxiang, who was known to be close to Xu, was also implicated. Subsequently, various social groups and overseas Chinese repeatedly appealed, and the Xiamen judge carefully investigated and confirmed that he had been falsely accused and granted bail. Since Mr. Chen Yanxiang has been cleared of the false accusation and granted bail, it is appropriate to quickly dismiss the case against him. Recently, it was heard that this case has been transferred to the Zhejiang Hangzhou Court for investigation. The government is cautious about these matters, and it seems unnecessary for us to dwell on them, especially as we live far away. However, considering that Mr. Chen and Mr. Xu were like-minded and shared the same ideals, and there has never been any resentment or conflict of interest between them, it is clear that there is no reason for anyone to cause death without a cause. This is very clear. When judging a person, one must look at their usual behavior. We, overseas Chinese, have carefully considered the situation and observed that Mr. Chen Yanxiang's usual behavior is trustworthy. Therefore, we have sent letters and telegrams to appeal on his behalf. Furthermore, Mr. Chen is currently the general manager of the Tongmei Road Company. This road was established entirely with overseas Chinese capital. If he is implicated in the Xu case and goes to Hangzhou to await trial, there will be no suitable person to take his place in road administration. We fear that the delay will inevitably hinder the progress of road administration, and the capital of overseas Chinese will be greatly affected. We have always admired our government's unwavering support for overseas Chinese investment and business ventures. Therefore, we earnestly request your court to investigate and adjudicate the Xu case impartially. Since Mr. Chen has been confirmed to have been falsely accused, it is appropriate to quickly dismiss the case against him so that road administration can be maintained and the innocent can avoid being implicated. This would fulfill the wishes of the overseas Chinese and be a virtuous act.

Frequent Kidnappings in Rural Suzhou: A few days ago, five bandits armed with handguns raided the home of Wang Ayi, a Shaoxing farmer in Tanqiu Village, Pingwang Township, Wujiang County, and kidnapped his 15-year-old grandson, Wang Tianyou. They left a ransom note demanding a large sum of money. Before leaving, they kidnapped the store owner Ma Wenxiang and his grandson Ma Yuekui. Gao Ying Case Extended for Three Months: The Supreme Court ruled on October 6 that the former San Francisco Vice-Consul Gao Ying and his secretary Sun Yuan's case involving the trafficking of opium should be reviewed by the court. The High Court believed that the case had international implications, so it was resolved to be handed over to the Criminal Division I, headed by Judge Lin Dawen. Judge Lin stated that the case required a thorough investigation of the evidence and could not be scheduled for trial in a short time. It is reported that it will be extended for three months. Once the evidence is clarified, a hearing will be scheduled, likely in January or February next year. Misunderstanding in Prison Investigation: Prison warden Wang Kaikai of Wujiang County was transferred from Qidong County only two months ago. After Wang took office, someone accused him of deducting prisoners' food rations. Earlier this month, the county magistrate of Wujiang, based on the accusation, sent Wu Guangxi to investigate the prison. At that time, Wu and the prison staff had a misunderstanding, leading to a conflict. The county magistrate immediately telegraphed the High Court to request instructions. President Lin, after receiving the telegram on the 8th of this month, appointed judicial committee member Yao Guozhang to conduct a thorough investigation. Committee member Yao returned to Suzhou yesterday to report the findings. According to the investigation, the situation at the time was indeed a misunderstanding between the two parties. Request to Reduce the Autumn Grain Tax Denied: The two county heads of Wu County convened local gentry to discuss and determine that 93% of the autumn grain harvest should be collected. The proposal was submitted to the Finance Department for approval. Yesterday (the 11th), the Finance Bureau issued an order stating that the autumn harvest in Suzhou and Changzhou counties was abundant, and most were collected in full. The situation in the county should be the same, and the full amount should be collected according to the new regulations. The request to reduce the collection by 7% was not approved. Frequent Banditry in Xishan: Recently, lake bandits have frequently occurred in the area of Lao Shushan near Xishan County, robbing ships and harassing people. Representatives of Workers Go to Nanjing to Petition: For the sake of the existence of the unions, the workers' associations of various industries in Suzhou and elsewhere specially sent representatives Shi Zhifan, Lu Jupo, and six others to Nanjing yesterday (the 11th) morning to petition the Fourth Plenary Session.

Wuxi 59

Patrol Officer Abuses Power to Snatch Bride

It is said that Gao Wende, a patrol officer of the Third Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau outside the South Gate of Wuxi, is inherently wicked and lustful. Recently, he became intimate with the sister of Xu Shunfa, a Yancheng native residing in the area. They lived together like husband and wife. However, Xu's sister had already been betrothed to Li Jiazhong, a fellow townsman, through a matchmaker years ago. Li, who was working in Shanghai, recently chose an auspicious day and came to Wuxi the day before yesterday to marry Xu's sister and bring her home for the wedding ceremony. Unexpectedly, at around 4 a.m. the next morning, Patrol Officer Gao Wende led two police officers and, together with Xu Shunfa, went to the Li's residence and forcibly took Xu's sister away. Afterwards, Li Jiazhong reported the incident to the Third Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau. The head of the sub-bureau, Wang Tingshu, immediately dispatched police officers to detain Patrol Officer Gao Wende, Xu Shunfa, and Xu's sister after receiving the report. Following a preliminary trial by Director Wang, Li Jiazhong was ordered to pay sixty-four yuan as compensation and provide six sets of clothing before taking Xu's sister back. Meanwhile, Patrol Officer Gao Wende was dismissed and released. Li, considering the sub-bureau head's judgment unjust, went to Zhenjiang to seek assistance from the secretary-general. A certain gentleman, upon learning of the matter, immediately sent a letter to the stationed Xianbing (military police) in Wuxi, requesting Jin Deyi to forward it to the Public Security Bureau for a thorough investigation. Director Wang Tingshu, seeing the situation was unfavorable, detained Xu Shunfa, Xu's sister, and Li Jiazhong and sent them to the General Bureau. Yesterday, they were transferred to the county government. It is heard that the court ordered Li Jiazhong to take leave, while Xu Shunfa and Xu's sister were ordered to provide bail. Due to the inability to obtain bail, they were temporarily detained.

The county government decided on four important cases. Yesterday, the county government of Wuxi held its 64th county administration meeting, resolving the following matters:

(1) Ni Jianye, the acting district chief of the 14th District, submitted a proposal to collect urgent Cao taxes, suggesting that the district office print temporary receipts to be issued by the Jia heads to the payers to prevent abuses. The proposal included a sample receipt and requested review. It was resolved to forward it to the Finance Bureau for review and response.

(2) Hou Dan and other students from Wuxi studying at the Jiangsu Provincial Police Academy submitted a request for a subsidy of fifty yuan per student per semester due to financial difficulties. It was resolved that the local finances were extremely strained, making it impossible to allocate funds.

(3) It was proposed that the county's banquet tax be verified and collected by the Finance Bureau. It was resolved to proceed accordingly.

(4) It was proposed to find a way to prevent local thugs from causing trouble on the Wuxi-Chengdu road due to the rickshaws there. It was resolved to task the 6th, 12th, and 3rd Sub-bureaus of the Public Security Bureau to dispatch police to patrol and strictly investigate and handle such incidents.

Brother and Sister-in-law Engage in Adultery and Abuse the First Wife

It is reported that A'Man, the sister of Zhang Jilin, a villager from the 14th 4th Tu in the 16th District (Wan'an City), was married to Pan Sandao from Panxiang. The couple had been harmonious since their marriage. However, recently, Pan became romantically involved with his sister-in-law, Mrs. Pan, and began to treat his first wife like an eyesore, constantly insulting and beating her, causing A'Man to be covered in bruises. The day before yesterday, Pan Sandao, for some unknown reason, summoned local ruffians Pan Wushi, Pan Alin, Pan Wuda, Gao Chou, etc., and used thick iron chains to lock A'Man on the coffin of his deceased father, denying her food and drink. The villagers, upon seeing this, were outraged and immediately reported to A'Man's brother, Zhang Jilin, who went to negotiate with Pan Sandao. After receiving the report, Director Xu immediately dispatched armed police to arrest them. Fengxian 60

Denying an Old Marriage, She Commits Suicide in Anger

It is reported that Zhenxiu, the daughter of Zhou Huajia, a Huizhou native residing in the east of Guojia Temple, was betrothed by her parents to Tianren, the son of Yu Fusheng, a fellow townsman who runs a meat shop in Minhang. However, Yu's son was unattractive and weak, while the daughter was young and beautiful and educated. Therefore, she was greatly dissatisfied with the marriage. Because the woman's father was a follower of the old ethics, he rejected her repeated requests for annulment. On November 1st, the woman suddenly learned that the wedding date was approaching and, fearing a grave mistake, she was forced to elope with her lover, a certain Mr. You (currently a teacher at a certain school), to show her determination. Unexpectedly, the news leaked, and her father found out and placed her under guard. The woman, unable to achieve her goal, hanged herself in shame and anger last night. Everyone far and near who heard the news mourned her.

Changshu 61

The Cloth Factory Building Suddenly Collapses, A Strange Noise Heard Outside the Factory

It is reported that in Taojia Village, near Hongqiao Temple outside the Dadongmen Gate in Changshu, the Jingfeng Cloth Factory, consisting of dozens of houses built by the Tao family nine years ago on remaining land, has been operating and producing a large quantity of goods on a daily basis. While work was in progress in the factory the day before yesterday, a loud noise was suddenly heard outside the factory trees, with a gust of wind circling the trees. The factory staff and workers, totaling several hundred people, all went outside to watch. However, an old woman and an eighteen-year-old female worker in the factory had stayed inside, diligently working on the project, and had not gone out. As the staff and workers went to look, they did not find anything. As they went to go back, a noise from the factory structure was suddenly heard, as the wood creaked. In an instant, the factory building collapsed, involving over thirty rooms. All of the wooden machines, as well as the upper and lower yarn threads, were pressed inside. The old woman and young female worker who had not gone out were also caught in the bricks and rubble. Upon becoming aware of the situation, people soon opened the rubble and rescued the two workers, but their bodies were covered in cuts and bruises. They were soon sent to the hospital for treatment, although there is not yet news of their lives. The estimated loss is approximately ten thousand gold. According to people who later discussed the incident, people were quite struck by the loud noise from the tree catastrophe.

Cai Yuanpei Visits Yushan

It is said that Cai Yuanpei, the president of the Academia Sinica, passed through Suzhou the day before yesterday and, along with Zhang Yi, came to Changshu to travel. They stayed at the Shimei Yushan Inn, where they were accompanied by former County Magistrate Pang Diancai and Ju Liangshi to visit scenic spots such as the Poshan Temple and the Sanfeng Temple in the North Mountain. However, the weather was not good, as fine rain was falling. Cai and others braved the rain and traveled by sedan chair.

A Boat Encountered Robbery Midway

It is reported that a boat from Tianzhuang Township in Changshu has been traveling daily to Jiangyin. The day before yesterday, when Kai Cheng sailed from Tianzhuang at around 5 a.m., before dawn, and passed through Yangku Weikan Zhuangqiao Port area, it suddenly encountered a pirate ship. The pirates, numbering about ten, stopped the boat and robbed it. The boat owner, Xu Fuquan, seeing the situation was not good, immediately steered along the bank and threw the cash package ashore. As the pirates boarded the boat to rob, they only stole clothes and silver dollars from the passengers. In total, it was estimated to be around eighty or ninety yuan.

Wu Xushi's Home in Baitangqiao Was Robbed

It is reported that Wu Xushi, a woman from Jinquan Place in Baitangqiao, Xupu Township in Jiangcheng District, is quite wealthy. Unexpectedly, the day before yesterday, more than ten robbers suddenly came at midnight, all holding handguns, sharp blades, and flashlights, and broke into the home of the clan. At the time, the Xu clan mother and daughter were fast asleep and were awakened upon hearing a noise. The robbers tied up the mother and daughter, and the head robber directed the group to overturn trunks and open chests, looting all the ornaments and silver dollars inside. It was then heard that people in the downstairs room were also robbed. Relatives Mr. Li and others were staying in the downstairs room at the time. The robbers entered the room and searched everywhere, and the silver dollars in the pockets of Mr. Li and others were also searched and looted. After the robbery, they went to the north. It is said that Wu Xushi's home was robbed because the family's daughter recently returned to her hometown from Wuxi to visit her mother, carrying trunks of clothing and goods, and therefore the robbers were coveting this.

Nantong 62

The Former Police Captain is Subjected to Military Law Adjudication

Yan Diannan, the former captain of the Nantong County Police Brigade, was corrupt and unlawful during his tenure. He has been arrested and detained in the Zhenjiang County Prison Detention Center. Chairman Ye of the Provincial Government has sent him to the Military Law Section of the Provincial Security Department for adjudication. Director Li ordered the County Government to summon Xu Hanru, the plaintiff and District Chief of the Eighteenth District, to the Provincial Office for questioning on the 18th of this month.

The Lusi Bandits were Repelled and Aftermath Arrangements Made

The sea bandits who occupied Lusi Sanjia Town have been repelled by the police and militia. Local organizations are now gathering to discuss the aftermath. Watchtowers have been set up at the harbor and cannons have been erected to guard against bandits. All the bandits' houses have been demolished.

The Joint Preservation of Land by Nantong, Changshu, and Jiangyin Counties

The collapse of the Liuhaisha Sandbank, jointly administered by Nantong, Changshu, and Jiangyin counties, is very serious. The Construction Bureaus of the three counties have jointly formulated measures to preserve the land, defining the area within 1,600 zhang from the riverbank as the scope for collecting preservation fees. Discussions are currently underway.

Page 10

Zhenjiang 63

A Farmer in Xiecun is Killed by Bandits

It is reported that Yuan Yousong, a farmer in Xiecun in the western part of Zhenjiang, about ten miles from Xiashu, was a family of modest means. At about 9 p.m. the night before last, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came, all armed with handguns. When entering the village, they first fired shots to show their power, and then used stones to break down the door. Gu, seeing that there were bandits, immediately climbed onto the roof and threw roof tiles at them. The bandits then fired two shots at the roof, killing Gu on the spot. Yuan's family has reported the incident to the county government and requested the garrisoning of troops for defense.

Another Incident of Assault by Cart Porters

It is said that cart porters at Xiaomatou assaulted each other over competition to carry Yi Chengzang's bags, resulting in multiple injuries. The Seventh Sub-bureau transferred the case to the court. Yesterday, the prosecutor opened the court for investigation and ordered Liu Dianliang and five others who were most seriously injured to be sent to the hospital for treatment. Liang Baozhu and nine others who were slightly injured were released on bail for medical treatment. The remaining five, such as Song Wenlin, were temporarily detained for further investigation.

The Sixth Division Deploys Troops to Gaozi to Suppress Bandits

The 9th and 11th Companies of the 31st Regiment of the 17th Brigade of the Sixth Division have been ordered to deploy to Gaozi to suppress bandits and will implement extending the Yangtze River Estuary Station.

The Yangtze River Estuary Station to be Extended

Due to the silting up of the Zhenjiang beach, ships cannot connect with the station, and many northbound passengers and goods are rerouted, causing the Zhenjiang commercial port to decline. The Chamber of Commerce previously submitted a request to the Ministry of Railways to extend the Yangtze River Estuary Station route or to build a branch line from the South Gate Station to Ganlu Port. It is now heard that the Ministry of Railways believes that the construction of the Ganlu Port route requires expanding the South Gate Station and the total cost is one million yuan. Whether the future freight income can offset the cost is still questionable and requires detailed planning before a decision can be made. It has ordered the Railway Bureau to extend the Yangtze River Estuary Station to Zhenjiangguan for a temporary remedy.

The Case of the Soldier Shot Solved

Regarding the incident of a soldier being shot in front of the Mingxing Cinema on Zhongshan Road the night before last, it is now known that the seriously injured soldier, Chen Chi, was carried to the Xiong Shengzhi Hospital, but due to his severe injuries, he died at 5 a.m. yesterday. Chen was a first-class soldier in the machine gun unit of the 3rd Battalion of the 31st Regiment of the 11th Brigade of the Sixth Division, and was from Zhejiang. At 10 a.m. yesterday, Chen Fu, the director of the Public Security Bureau of the provincial capital, and Wang Chen, the battalion commander of the 3rd Battalion of the Sixth Division, went to the scene of the incident in front of the Mingxing Cinema to investigate the truth. It was completed at 11 a.m. It is heard that the incident was purely a misunderstanding and a decision has been made on how to handle it: (1) Punish the shooter (2) Raise funds to comfort the family of the deceased (3) Hold a memorial meeting at a set time. It is said that Xie Zhouzong, Ma Jiagan, Xu Zongpu, and three other lightly injured soldiers are all fine.

Yangzhou 64

Jiangdu New Chamber of Commerce Elects Officers

The Jiangdu County Chamber of Commerce held its first members' representative meeting in the assembly hall of the association at 9:00 a.m. on the 10th. As a result of the election, Wang Jingting, Guo Lanshi, Dai Jingshan, Sun Yaozhang, Hu Xinyao, Huang Yizhi, Ling Tangbo, Luo Zhizhi, Zhu Zhusun, Zhao Boang, Teng Yizhai, Shi Ruixin, Xia Xiaocen, Jiang Yunqiu, and Pan Songping, a total of fifteen people, were elected as executive members, while Zhao Haishan, Cao Bingnan, Zhao Pinchchen, Liu Lushu, Wu Runzhi, Hua Jingshu, and Song Shenzhi, seven people, were elected as supervisory members.

New and Old Organizing Committee Hold a Meeting to Re-elect New Members

The three organizing members of the Jiangdu Party Organizing Committee, Zhu, Hu, and Chen, arrived in Yangzhou on the 9th and held the 57th committee meeting at 9:00 a.m. on the 10th to discuss proposals. After the vote, Wang Lu was elected as the executive committee member, Chen Shouyan supervised the handover of the secretariat, Tang Shou supervised the handover of the propaganda department, Shi Youxiang supervised the handover of the organization department, and Wang Lu supervised the handover of the training department. Tang Shou and Chen Shouyan were appointed as economic review committee members of the association, and it was decided that the staff of the association are absolutely not allowed to hold concurrent positions.

Jiangyin 65

Bandits from Jingjiang County Arrested in Cheng

The Jingjiang County Detective Team, acting on a tip that wanted bandits had arrived in Cheng from Shanghai, dispatched sixteen plainclothes detectives across the river on the 9th. At approximately 3:00 p.m., they apprehended five bandits, Cai Desheng, Fang Wenbin, Cao Junqing, Zhu Cheng, and Lu Guiyan, at Du Yongxing's Inn in Huangtian Port. That evening, they were escorted to Jiangjiang County for interrogation.

The Veterans' Hospital is Reorganized; Can be Merged Soon

The County Organizing Committee, together with various organizations and groups, had telegraphed the Commander-in-Chief, stating that since the 25-bed hospital established in Jiangyin had treated more than ten wounded soldiers sent in April, the financial burden, including previous gratuities, was unsustainable. As the personnel who had come to Cheng had already gradually recovered, they requested that orders be issued promptly for them to return to their units and to close the hospital. On the 9th, a telegram was received from the Headquarters, stating that once the large number of wounded soldiers had been processed for return to their units, the hospital could be reorganized and closed.

A Clerk Took His Own Life by Jumping into the River Due to Embezzlement

Zhang Shiqing, a clerk at the Huangtang Yimao branch of the Qingyang Yufeng Cloth Store, who was originally from the Xiannvmiao River Ferry in Yangzhou, embezzled the store’s money due to family difficulties and his wife’s illness. After this was discovered by the manager, Shen Zhiqing, Zhang Shiqing had been falsely accused by his friend of having dissipated the missing funds. He could not deal with the situation, and embracing a world-weary sentiment, he traveled to Yang on the sixth day of the ninth lunar month on a fourth-class train, arriving in Shanghai and staying at the Zhonghua Small Hotel. On the 17th, he went to Wusong Fort, Taiwan, and jumped into the river, killing himself. Yesterday, Xue Chan, a friend of Zhang from Jiangsheng, received a suicide note Zhang sent from Shanghai, and only then did he learn the news of his suicide.

Danyang 66

Communist Yin Fubao Arrested

It is reported that Yin Fubao, from Xiashu Township in Shangde City, was previously reported for having communist suspicions and was wanted by the county government without success. Recently, Yin secretly returned to his hometown and was discovered by Gu Weibang and others from Xinfeng Township, who secretly reported it to the county magistrate Shen. County Magistrate Shen specifically ordered the police to arrest and interrogate the suspect.

Banditry Revives in the West of the County

It is reported that small groups of bandits have been found in the western part of the county, which borders Zhenjiang, looting and extorting at times. Recently, several people have been abducted from Fengcun and Caojia Village, Zhenjiang. Residents of the Zhenjiang border area have fled to Danyang one after another. It is also heard that the bandits have publicly threatened to go to Xinnan Village to loot and eat their fill on a specific date. County Magistrate Shen, upon receiving the report, has ordered the police to go and provide protection.

Huzhou 67

The Patrol Team Exchanges Fire with Bandits in Zhangcun

It is reported that the patrol team of the Third District of the Nanxun Water Police in Huzhou arrested four bandits in the western countryside some days ago. They immediately questioned the bandits, who confessed that all the firearms were hidden near the empty tomb near the junction of Shiyang and Zhangcun. The team, according to the confession, immediately dispatched the former squad leader and fourteen police officers, along with the four bandits they had captured, to search on the morning of the 9th. Unexpectedly, as they were about to arrive at the place, a bandit ship suddenly came with more than ten bandits, each holding firearms, to pick up the bandit prisoners. At this time, the former squad leader, fearing that the bandit prisoners would be taken away, first executed the four bandits and then engaged in a battle with the incoming bandits. After an hour of fighting, because there were few soldiers and many bandits, two police officers were injured and the bandits also retreated. They captured a bandit ship and four guns.

A Widow Loses Her Body and Is Involved in Lawsuit

It is reported that Wu Chunsheng, an elderly man from Shujiawan, outside the North Gate, has a son, Ruizhi, who died of illness last year. The family consists of his widowed daughter-in-law, Mrs. Yang, who is not yet thirty years old and has a daughter. Because the family is poor and struggling to make ends meet, there is talk of her remarrying. A neighbor, a certain Shen, acted as matchmaker and arranged for her to marry a certain Zhang from the same village. However, Wu Chunsheng demanded an excessive bride price, and the marriage did not materialize. Because her widowed daughter-in-law believed that her father-in-law was demanding too much, she took her young daughter and left the house on the night before last, her whereabouts unknown. Wu, in a fit of anxiety, seized Shen and demanded the person, or else he would report to the police to investigate the abduction. The outcome of the discussion is yet unknown.

Pinghu 68

The Bandit Zhou Asheng is Arrested

It is reported that yesterday (the 9th) morning, more than ten fully armed bandits, including Zhou Asheng and Yang Ayin, the lieutenants of the gangster Taibao Ashu, came to Weiqian Town in the east of the county, and stayed in the vicinity of the Dongshi area. At around 12:00, many police officers of the Jiangsu Water Police led by Tan Meisheng, all dressed in civilian clothes, followed and arrived in the town. Zhou Asheng was smoking in the Swallow's Nest opened by A Quan. After learning this, each of the detectives bravely charged in with box cannons and arrested Zhou. Most of the other bandits were tasting tea in the teahouse and fled without a trace upon hearing the alarm. As a result, only one bandit, Zhou, was captured. It is said that Zhou was formerly a carpenter, but now he has joined Taibao Ashu's gang and is quite strong.

Shen Shoufu Was Killed by Bandits

It is said that Shen Shoufu from Xielefang was an assistant to the nuclear square guard Guo Quanhe. Three years ago, Liu Dexing stole someone's farm cattle and Shen arrested Liu and sent him to the county for a sentence of four months' imprisonment. This spring, Liu joined the bandit party when the bandits robbed Xinhui, and declared that he would kill Shen to avenge the old hatred. At the beginning of last month, the bandit Liu sneaked back to the village and was almost captured by the local guards. Afterwards, Liu suspected that Shen had reported him, and his hatred deepened. At about 10 p.m. on the 5th, Shen was sipping tea at A Lai's small teahouse when Liu suddenly broke in with a wooden-cased gun. Shoufu, seeing that the situation was not good, was about to flee, but Liu dragged him out of the teahouse and shot Shen five times in a row next to the nearby small beach. Fu Shou was killed on the spot. Liu, seeing that his goal had been achieved, led more than ten members of his gang and fled. The family of Shen and the village elders have reported to the county for investigation.

Hangzhou 69

Planning to Build Public Docks Across the Province

The Provincial Navigation Bureau has discussed the construction of public docks, and it has now been decided to select twenty sites for construction. The Construction Department has prescribed a measurement fee, with a total cost of 3,968 yuan. A measurement team has been organized to proceed in three routes: the first route is from Hangzhou via Wenjiayu, Linpu, Tonglu, Yandongguan to Lanluo; the second route is from Hangzhou via Gongchen Bridge, Tanglou, Jiaxing, Pinghu to Wuxing; the third route is from Hangzhou to Shanghai to Dinghai, Shenjiamen, Caotuo, Zhenhai, Linhai, Yongjia, Qingtian, Yuhuan, Kanmen to Jinqing Port. Once the survey plan is completed, construction will begin.

Xiaoshan 70

A Husband and Wife Quarrel and Commit Suicide Together

It is reported that Zhou Xichuan, a farmer from Xizhou, outside the South Gate of Xiaoshan, had been at odds with his wife. On the night of the 9th, they quarreled again. The wife, feeling angry and unbearable, threw herself into the river to die. She was pulled out by bystanders, but she had already died. Her husband, because his wife had committed suicide, also hanged himself at midnight. By the morning of the 10th, he had also died. The situation was very tragic.

The West Gate County Road is Completed

It is reported that the section of the county road from Xiaoshan Xixing to the West Gate was decided to be constructed by the County Administration Council. Now, the section from the West Gate to the Laoyu Temple has been completed. The section from Xixing to Xiaoyue Temple will also be under construction in about a month and can be fully completed by the New Year's Day of the 20th year (of the Republic of China).

Ruian 71

The Case of Counterfeit Silver Coins in Ruian County Suffers a Setback

It is reported that a case of private counterfeiting of silver coins occurred in the Baodi area of Ruian County in June of this year. The perpetrators were Dai Riming, Dai Richou, Li Desheng, and Dai Jianfan. The incident was discovered and reported by Dai Xiaolan, Dai Yezhi, and Dai Riren, residents of the area, to Sun Yu, the captain of the anti-smuggling battalion. The people and the evidence were seized. Then, a certain Dai Xuebo stepped in to mediate and gave the anti-smuggling battalion 1,400 yuan. Later, Dai Xiaolan and others learned of this. Considering that the case was of great importance and should be severely punished by the judicial authorities, they believed that the anti-smuggling battalion had dared to take bribes and let go of the perpetrators, which was illegal. They immediately filed a lawsuit with the Ruian Court. The court immediately dispatched police to arrest the defendants, but the defendants had all fled upon hearing the news. The captain of the anti-smuggling battalion was also dismissed and fled with the stolen goods. The case was suspended. Unexpectedly, the defendants spared no expense in secretly engaging people to make connections and lobby everywhere, but all failed to achieve their goals. Last month, the judge in charge of the case was suddenly transferred, and a certain Zhou succeeded him. The defendants thought there was an opportunity and engaged local gentry Mr. Jiang to secretly lobby Judge Zhou with a large sum of money. Judge Zhou suddenly ordered the plaintiffs Dai Xiaolan, Ye Zhi, or Riren to appear in court on the 28th of last month. Without questioning the situation, he ordered them to pay a cash bail of 500 yuan. Dai and others were in the position of plaintiffs, and the defendants had all fled. The plaintiffs should not be detained and charged innocently. It is heard that they have appealed to the higher court to clarify the truth.

Luhe 72

The Dispute over the Contracting of Juzizhou Island

Juzizhou Island is originally a public property of Luhe and Jiangpu counties. All charitable undertakings rely on it. It is now heard that Ye Xin has contracted over 900 acres of new beach on the island from the Sandfield Bureau. People from Pu and Lu counties, upon learning of this, unanimously opposed it and urged the competent authorities to fight for their rights. Not an inch of local public property should be lost.

The Cotton Industry Strike

Although the number of cotton workers in Luhe is less than one hundred, many cotton workers from Jiangpu, Nanjing, Yizheng, Chuzhou, and other counties are from Luhe County. Therefore, the cotton workers of each county are under the control of Luhe. A month ago, the cotton workers here requested an increase in wages and went on strike once. As a result, wages were increased and work resumed. Unexpectedly, because the wages in other counties are now higher than those in Luhe, a second strike occurred on the 5th of this month. The capitalists, because the winter season is approaching and they urgently need goods, had no choice but to accept the workers' conditions and resume work as usual on the 8th of this month.

Incoming Letters

Letter from the Liyang Association in Beijing 73

To the Editor,

Regarding the report of the Liyang Coverup and Corruption Case in the Local News section of your esteemed newspaper on the 8th of this month, there are many inaccuracies regarding our association. After investigation, the representatives of our association who went to the provincial government to petition did not make such a claim. They only requested that the provincial government organize a special court to publicly try and severely punish the perpetrators of the case and the corrupt officials of the Kuomintang Party headquarters who initiated the coverup, in order to uphold the reputation of the Party. As for transferring the perpetrators to the judiciary for investigation, it is completely untrue and is what our association opposes the most. Fearing that the outside world may misunderstand due to unclear information, we specially send this letter for correction and request your understanding.

Respectfully,

The Liyang Association in Beijing, November 11

Education News

Important News

The Student Committee Rejects Mediation 74

(Tokyo Electric News, 11th) The Student Union Committee of Waseda University held a meeting yesterday afternoon and put the mediation proposal of Nakano Seigo to a vote. After the split vote, the committee decided to reject the proposal. Five members of the Control Department Committee visited Nakano to inform him of the rejection. Nakano said that the Control Department was too irresponsible to endorse the mediation proposal and declared that he would no longer mediate. Students in the political science department in grades two and three who supported the mediation proposal withdrew from the union. Students in the science and engineering departments decided to start classes from today. The situation on the student side is gradually becoming chaotic.

The Education Community of Fengxian County Retains Zhuang Yijian 75

Since the Provincial Government passed a motion in the 3rd, 4th, and 5th meetings to appoint Song Binggong as the Director of the Education Bureau, the 6th Standing Committee of the County Education Association resolved unanimously to reject the motion. A telegram has been found, the contents of which are transcribed below:

To Chen, Director of the Education Department in Zhenjiang: We have recently read in the newspapers that the Provincial Government has passed a motion to appoint Song Binggong to succeed the Director of the County Education Bureau. We are deeply puzzled by this news. The current Director, Zhuang Yijian, has been diligent in his work and has spared no effort in planning and implementing education throughout the county. He has been dedicated to his duties and is well-liked by the public. A sudden change may cause disputes. Article 17 of the revised County Organization Law promulgated by the National Government in July of this year stipulates that the Director of each County Education Bureau should be selected by the County Magistrate from qualified candidates after examination and submitted for approval. Article 7 of the regulations on the organization of County Education Bureaus promulgated by your department also has the same provision. If it is necessary to change the Director of the County Education Bureau, the selection procedure by the County Magistrate should be followed to comply with the law. Moreover, Song Binggong is a native of another county and is completely unfamiliar with the educational situation in the county. Taking on this position suddenly will make it difficult to achieve results due to the lack of familiarity with the people and the place. We believe that whether the Director is well-suited for the job is crucial to the future of education, and we believe that there is no need to change the current Director. We hereby submit a telegram respectfully requesting your department to review it and promptly submit it to the Provincial Government to withdraw the order, so as to avoid disputes and comfort the public. The entire Executive Committee of the Fengxian County Education Association bows in unison.

Local

The First District Party Headquarters Opposes the Establishment of an Education Department 76

The Nationalist Society's First District Party Headquarters in this city issued a declaration opposing the establishment of an education department by the Municipal Council, stating that the Shanghai concessions have existed for over eighty years. During these eighty years, imperialists have used them to realize their economic and cultural aggression. The impact has led to the daily collapse of China's economic state, and the people's livelihood has become increasingly difficult. Disturbances, robberies, disasters, and internal wars, all kinds of unfortunate phenomena occur from time to time within the country. For the sake of expanding their own interests, imperialists do not care about the life or death of China. They cruelly and brutally oppress the Chinese people, who are living in a dreamlike state, awakening from intoxication to awareness, and uniting together like scattered sand. The nationalist movement has swept the country. For forty years, the development of this movement has been dissatisfied with the government, which led to its overthrow, and the Republic of China was born. Although the nationalist movement only seeks the survival of the nation and does not resist oppression, this obstacle to national survival means the imperialist nationalist movement will never succeed. Therefore, in recent years, China's nationalist movement has shifted from internally overthrowing the Manchu government to externally overthrowing imperialism. In this nationalist movement, there is no day without struggle. We deeply recognize that the only condition for this movement to exert sustained force is to awaken national consciousness and cultivate national consciousness. We have no doubt that the way to awaken and cultivate this national consciousness lies in education. In the process of imperialists invading weak nations, they also pay attention to cultural aggression. They recognize that the only driving force for undermining and weakening national movements, which is national consciousness, requires the use of cultural aggression as a tool. The headquarters of imperialist cultural aggression in China, the missionary schools, have survived and expanded for nearly a hundred years under the protection of unequal treaties. The deep-rooted foundation they have built makes us astonished and frightened. The students cultivated in this cultural aggression headquarters, what are they like? Most of their thoughts are numb, and their national consciousness has long been destroyed. Social dancing intoxicates their entire lives. All their actions indicate that they are willing to be meritorious servants of imperialist economic aggression. Imperialists have cultivated a land full of cultural aggression and meritorious servants of economic aggression, young people with weakened thoughts. They are not satisfied, and they believe that they should further their aggression. The Shanghai Public Concession Municipal Council recently established an education department to act out its vicious means of cultural aggression and eliminate our national consciousness. The Education Department is the highest educational administrative organ of the Republic of China. Within the territory of the Republic of China, no second education department is allowed to exist, and the Shanghai Public Concession is not allowed to have similar organizations to realize its cultural aggression and eliminate national consciousness. The party headquarters in this district, in response to the Municipal Council's contempt for China's sovereignty and insult to the people of the whole country, in addition to quietly awaiting the government to lodge a serious protest, has no choice but to vigorously oppose it. It also hopes that the people of the whole country will recognize the importance of this move amid the advancement of imperialist cultural aggression, and jointly resist it, and then eliminate the concessions produced by unequal treaties, which are tools of this cultural aggression, in order to seek the survival of our nation. This declaration is hereby made.

Municipal Education Bureau's Small Problem Experiment Conference 77

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's Research Department believes that educational experiments have necessary methods to improve education and enhance educational efficiency. In addition to conducting educational experiments on gifted children at home, it has recently been conducting small problem experiments. Fourteen schools in Xicheng Sheng have been selected as experimental schools. The first meeting was held on October 14th, and the second meeting was held a few days ago. Zhao Lüqing, Xu Jiongqian, Xi An, Tan Panxin, Chen Yi, Xu Yaqian, Bo Jun, Xu Guangguang, Zong Tingying, Wan Jingzhang, Sheng Shuyun, Wang Lingcheng, Xiong Ruiting, Chen Bingqian, etc. attended. Ding Zhongguan chaired the meeting, and Zhao Lüqing took the minutes. After reporting, the following discussions were held: (1) Determining the small problems that can be used for experimentation and the school cases. It was resolved to select based on the experimental problems submitted by Fu Jiao and various schools, and the following were selected separately: (1) Which is more effective, composition topics or no composition topics (Wuben Attached Elementary School)? (2) Which is more suitable for low-grade writing tools, hard pens and hard paper or soft pens and soft paper (Qiujiang)? (3) What is the efficiency of calligraphy tracing and copying in the third grade (Wanfu)? (4) Which is better, regular or irregular calligraphy practice (Qiehua)? (5) Which is better in the third grade teaching inspection results, the radical character search method or the four-corner character search method (Yangzheng)? (6) Which is more convenient for beginners to check the dictionary, the radical character search method or the head and tail number character search method (Qiuzhi)? (7) Which is more effective, scheduled writing or impromptu writing (Xicheng)? (8) Which is better, the four-corner character search method or the head and tail number character search method (Bicheng)? (9) Experiment on specific methods of silent reading practice in higher grades (McCall) (Jingzhong Attached Elementary School). (10) Which is more effective in teaching first grade arithmetic, separate learning of the four operations or mixed teaching of the four operations (Shihua)? (11) Which is better, graded or ungraded advanced composition (using symbols) (Longde)? (12) In the second grade, what is the effect of half the time spent on silent reading and half the time spent on reading aloud, and silent reading accounting for one-third and reading aloud accounting for two-thirds (undecided)? (13) Which is more effective, correcting errors in composition by understanding or repeated practice (undecided)? (14) In teaching ninth grade arithmetic, which is better, 30 minutes at a time for six times or 45 minutes at a time for four times (Meixi)? The following questions were resolved to be retained: (1) In middle grades, which is more effective, having teachers demonstrate and students copy familiar characters or allowing students to copy freely (2) Which is more effective, skimming or glancing (3) Comparative experiment of surgical learning procedures. (4) In teaching abacus, which is more economical and effective, starting from teaching the complete formula without any songs or starting from the application and teaching the songs separately as needed during the application? The following questions were designated as research topics: (1) What size of grid paper is most suitable for beginners to write (proposed by the Education Bureau)? (2) The relationship between children's errors and the sound, shape, and meaning of characters (proposed by Jiangde)? (3) The relationship between silent reading speed and comprehension (proposed by Jiangde)? (4) Research on art appreciation of elementary school children (proposed by Wuben Attached Elementary School)? (5) Which is more effective, direct or indirect batch editing of notes in each subject (proposed by Shihua)? (6) In which grade should phonetic symbols be taught (proposed by Xicheng)? (2) How should the problems for each person's research be managed? It was resolved to be discussed at the next meeting. (3) It was resolved to pass the draft experimental plan for the small problems undertaken by each school to be submitted for discussion before the next meeting. (4) It was resolved to have the Education Bureau separately notify the unrecognized experimental topics of each school.

The Shanghai Private Schools of the Recovering Concession Education Rights Promotion Association held an autumn dinner party a few days ago. Recent News of the Nanyang Medical College Storm 79

News from the Student Union of Nanyang Medical College: When the National Revolutionary Army recovered Shanghai in 1927, when it was time to recover educational rights, the principal of the school, the Japanese Tsunomiya Hiroshi, resigned. The School Affairs Maintenance Committee elected Wu Zongqing as the principal. In 1928, the school began to be established. Long before Wu Zongqing succeeded as principal for a year, the school and hospital equipment in the era of the Japanese Tsunomiya Hiroshi were very impressive, such as the bacterial practice room. All kinds of bacterial cultures should have everything. The affiliated hospital was in charge of the chief professor. The practice materials were very abundant. Now the bacterial practice room is covered with dust, and the practice materials are brought by the professor in private. Only one graduate of the school serves as a doctor in the affiliated hospital. There are very few patients every day. The internal situation of the school is very different from before. Since the beginning of this semester, the students' general assembly has proposed four minimum improvement plans, requiring Wu to adopt them. Wu initially agreed to convene a joint meeting to solve the problem, and then suspended the meeting in his personal capacity, while expelling eight executive committee members of the student union. These eight expelled people were the representatives that Wu invited to participate in the joint meeting.

Jinan Opens Exhibition and Sports Meet 80

National Jinan University prepared various commemorative activities a few days ago in advance for today's birthday of the founding father. The ceremony was held in Zhiyuan Hall at 9:00 a.m. At the same time, the representatives of the first Nanyang Overseas Chinese Education Conference presented a commemorative statue to President Zheng to comfort the Scout Nan You Walking Team, and opened a chrysanthemum exhibition, autumn sports meet, and Nan You Team goods exhibition. The team brought back many rare and bizarre local products from Nanyang, as well as various photos and inscriptions from people from various places, which were open to the public for viewing. In addition, the first directly affiliated district branch will also hold a celebration of the Prime Minister's birthday at the school at 2:00 p.m., and prepare for the second swearing-in ceremony for party members.

Sports

Municipal Elementary School Joint Sports Meet 81

Opening at 9:00 a.m. today. The annual Municipal Elementary School Joint Sports Meet opened at the Municipal Public Sports Field No. 1 at 9:00 a.m. today. A total of 84 schools participated. The students of each school must form a team at 8:30 a.m. The layout of the venue was completed the day before. The rostrum is located in the north of the runway with simple furnishings. A couplet is hung in front of it: [Those who cheer up their spirits, see who achieves the true results of sports in three days, and continue to train for ten years to become healthy citizens of China.] The seats of each school are arranged around the bamboo fence outside the running track. The seats for guests are located in the east of the running track. The resting place for male athletes is in the gymnasium, and the resting place for female athletes is in the small house west of the gymnasium. The resting place for the Scouts is in the tennis court, and the nursing station is under the grape trellis. The mayor and Xu, the director of the Education Bureau, have specially made awards to encourage those with excellent group performance and individual competition results. Many organizations, groups, and individuals also donate awards to promote the event. The order of the venue on the 12th and 13th will be maintained by the East Asia Sports Scout, and on the 14th by the China Sports School Scout. Free Talk

Dismissed with a Smile 90

— Hai Ke

Speaker (speaking in public): We are born in this world and must use our own strength to deal with everything. We must never rely on others. Therefore, whenever something comes to you, you must do it yourself.

A listener (standing up and questioning): Sir, then when your hair grows, do you cut and groom it yourself?

A: I think talking is the cheapest thing in the world, and it doesn't cost any money.

B: Who told you that talking costs money?

A: The day before yesterday, I went to see a lawyer to discuss something, and he actually asked me for five taels of silver for the conversation fee. Shanghai is really unaffordable to live in.

A: Military officer, I heard that you have experienced hundreds of battles and were able to return safely thanks to being rescued by an enemy officer. Is that true?

B: Military officer: Yes, that's right.

A: Military officer: This enemy officer is very respectable. I wonder what the situation was like.

B: Military officer: I took the initiative to kill him first, and he didn't have time to kill me, so he saved my life. A: I had to buy everything myself before I got married.

B: What happened now that you're married?

A: My wife buys and uses everything, and I don't even have money to buy anything myself.

Birthdays and National Humiliation 91

— Huang Yingdai

It has been sixty-four years since the birth of the Premier. Today is the Premier's birthday. If there had been no Premier's birth on this day, then our Chinese compatriots would still be oppressed under the autocratic government of the Manchu Qing Dynasty. The country would not be a country, and the people would not be the people, not knowing where to turn. Therefore, it goes without saying that today is a day worthy of our celebration. Recalling the Premier's lifelong energy devoted to the revolutionary cause, running for forty years, experiencing ten failures, but his will was not diminished. By knowing before others, awakening those who know later, and awakening those who awaken later, we were able to understand the corruption of the Qing government and the awesomeness of imperialism. A group rose up in revolution, and the Republic of China was established.

Today, we only know it as the Premier's birthday, but we do not know that it is also a period of national humiliation. In the Sino-Japanese War, the old and large China was defeated by the small Eastern Neighbor. As a result, our country's weakness was completely exposed. Seeing that Japan had gained considerable benefits, various countries greatly advocated their open-door policy and the principle of equal benefit, and all came to seize various rights. First, Russia, having threatened the return of Liaodong with success, again cited the previous example and demanded land from our country as a reward. The Qing government did not dare to refuse and sent Li Hongzhang to Russia, allowing Russia to have railway construction rights and mining rights in the three eastern provinces, and to lease Jiaozhou Bay as a naval port. Unexpectedly, the matter was learned by the Germans, who used the killing of German missionaries in Caozhou, Shandong, as a pretext to suddenly send warships to Jiaozhou Bay and forcibly lease it for a period of ninety-nine years, and obtain the construction rights of the Jiaoji Railway and mining rights within a hundred miles along the road. Russia's Jiaozhou Bay was occupied by Germany, so it revised a new treaty with our country and forcibly leased Lushun and Dalian for a period of twenty-five years. The British advocated the principle of naval equality and demanded the lease of Weihaiwei for a lease period similar to Lushun and Dalian. The French followed the example of the French and Germans, sending warships into Guangzhou Bay and forcibly leasing it for a lease period similar to Jiaozhou Bay. The British, seeing this, again used the excuse of the balance of power to demand the lease of land opposite Hong Kong to expand the old occupied Kowloon. The lease period was also like Guangzhou Bay. Since then, important ports have been leased by foreigners, and the national defense has been unable to be completely secure.

The day of the signing of the Guangzhou Bay treaty was the twelfth day of the eleventh month of the twenty-fifth year of Guangxu. It is a bay in the South China Sea, east of the Leizhou Peninsula. The entrance to the bay has Zhanchuan Island, dividing the mouth into two, a natural formation. However, the port is narrow and difficult to accommodate large ships. In the twenty-fourth year of Guangxu in the Qing Dynasty, it was occupied by the French. In the twenty-fifth year, a treaty was signed allowing it to be leased for a period of ninety-nine years. Now it is directly under the supervision of the Annam Governor-General. Therefore, today is both the Premier's birthday and the anniversary of the national humiliation of the Guangzhou Bay lease. We should not forget national humiliation while celebrating.

The Same Kind of Playing 92

— Zheng

Mr. Yu Rizhang said one day that foreigners often develop a fondness for sports, while Chinese people think that scholars should be gentle and refined, so they often cannot sustain their energy after middle age. Foreigners, because they have the habit of sports, still play golf in their old age even if they cannot do strenuous exercise. Chinese old people, however, go to play mahjong. The same kind of playing shortens the lives of Chinese people considerably.

Mourning the Passing of Tian Ziqin, a Disciple of the Law 93

— Wuwei Anzhu

Mr. Tian Ziqin of Qichun, named Tong, was famous throughout the world. I first met him at the seat of Mr. Pang Qingcheng of Wuxing. In the early summer of last year, Elder Qing invited us to a gathering at his Shanghai residence. Besides Mr. Tian, those present included Chen Shaobai, Xu Jingren, Shi Yiting, Hu Puan, and Ye Huijun. Mr. Tian's eloquence was particularly strong. After the banquet, he still spoke at length about national affairs, saying that he would vow to save the country with writing and mentioned plans to publish the Taiping Magazine. Later, I had the occasion to be invited to see him on several matters, and we visited each other frequently. In the third month of late spring, I had just returned to Shanghai from Qingdao and met Elder Qing. He told me that Mr. Tian had been admitted to the hospital with severe abdominal pain. The doctor diagnosed the disease as cancer. Both the late Premier and Liang Rengong, as well as Fa Nala Weng, all died from this incurable disease. Furthermore, great men and writers of China and the West have often lost their lives to this disease. Could it be that excessive mental effort and anxiety have led to this illness?

Elder Qing once showed me Mr. Tian's written description of his illness, written while he was in the hospital. At that time, because the pain was unbearable, he was reluctant to speak and used writing instead. It is what is now printed in the obituary. Elder Qing also said that Mr. Tian's illness had improved slightly, and the doctor said there were signs of recovery, but it was aggravated by overeating, which ultimately harmed his life. It is truly regrettable. I recall that when Su Manshu was ill, Elder Qing said that he also visited him every day. One day, there were signs of recovery, but the illness worsened and he died due to dietary indiscretion. Although the great events of life and death seem to be predetermined, one must be cautious about illness entering through the mouth. Whenever I think of the saying that "talented writers often have unfortunate lives, and demons like to harass people who are too clever," I cannot help but sigh for him.

On the second day of this month, Mr. Tian's family and friends held a memorial service for him at Chongfa Temple in Shanghai. I drove there at eleven o'clock. Mayor Zhang Yuejun came to offer condolences on behalf of the National Government, wearing only casual clothes. When I entered, I did not have time to sign my name because of the crowd. I saw a woman in plain clothes, about forty years old, standing beside the coffin. Her expression was very sad. A certain gentleman told me that this was Madam Juésheng, and she was also a grieving person. The hall was the temple's guest room. A lifelike portrait of Mr. Tian was hung in the center. The outer periphery of the colorful flower pavilion was adorned with fresh flowers, interspersed with yellow and white autumn chrysanthemums, which added to the faint purity and strength of character, just like Mr. Tian's personality. A white cloth curtain was hung outside, with a horizontal plaque with the four characters "Sound of Autumn Still There." Above the plaque was a couplet from the National Government: [Integrity unmatched, morality and economics unmatched] If Heaven had granted him more years, he would have surely made rain for the people. A biography in Confucian circles, a biography as a literary knight-errant. The public is originally immortal, willing to grow old in poverty on the Huangpu River.] The words are truly appropriate, and the parallelism between "the people" and "the Huangpu River" is also skillful. The blue satin memorial banners from Chairman Chiang were hung on the left and right sides of the couplet, with [Great Aspirations and Extraordinary Talent] on the left and [Name Survives Immortality] on the right. Chairman Chiang's elegiac couplet was hung on the large pillar, [Revolution promoted the enlightened, writing strategies for peace.] I deeply regret that Mr. Tian's self-edited Taiping Magazine was discontinued after three issues. Now that Mr. Tian is gone, there will be no one who can tell the revolutionary anecdotes recorded in Taiping that Mr. Tian had in his heart. In addition, there were thousands of elegiac couplets and memorial banners, with no space left in the two side rooms from the temple gate to the left and right of the altar. The sounds of drums and music in the hall competed to play mournful tunes that echoed around the beams. The plain carriages and white horses were endless, unable to overcome the pain of the loss of both the person and the music.

Impressions of West Lake 94

(6) Wisdom Sword

The boat arrived at Pinghu Qiuyue. After landing, I walked along the west road and arrived at Luoyuan, where the National Academy of Art is located. I sent a note asking someone to show me around. A certain gentleman in the academy guided me through the various studios. Among the teachers, I admired a large oil painting by Lin Fengmian. It was wide, about the size of a hall, and depicted several peasant women and children, each with a look of hesitation on their faces. Lin's paintings are majestic and colorful, and this painting is especially sufficient to express his character. The academy building is very simple, but the workmanship and materials seem to be quite expensive. It originally belonged to the British couple Hartung. Today, the National Academy of Art uses it. Leaving Luoyuan, I took a walk through the Wenlan Pavilion and Zhongshan Park. After the park is Gushan. I climbed it and looked out at the outer lake, the atmosphere was refreshing and incomparable. Passing Zhongshan Park, I arrived at Xiling Seal Society. As soon as I entered, I smelled the strong fragrance of osmanthus. My sleeves smelled as if there was a clear fragrance assaulting me. At the Seal Society, I bought a box of seal ink. I went further to the Sizhao Pavilion. This is the highest point on Gushan. I drank tea here for a while. The lake view was on the table, making me reluctant to leave. Behind the pavilion, on the cliffs, a small bronze statue of Mr. Wu Changshuo is planted, with many inscriptions by celebrities on both sides. Leaving Xiling Seal Society, I went to Guanghua Temple to see the Liuquan Spring. A porter followed me, asking if I would like to visit the Yue Temple. He also persuaded me to have a drink at Lou Wai Lou. I disliked it and ordered him to take me to the pier in front of Yue Temple. I would then take a boat to visit Yuquan.

Qinglian Temple is located north of Xiangu Mountain. Yuquan is inside it. I took a rickshaw there in the evening. After entering the mountain gate, I saw a light cloud filling the mountain like smoke, gently rippling. The mountain road was extremely desolate. There were many ruins and tombs on both sides. The rickshaw puller was old and panted as he walked. I stopped him from going further. It seemed that there was an old man directing the masons to repair the wall in the cemetery of the painter Tao Yuanqing. Going further, I saw a tomb with the words "Tomb of Lin Xiaohong of Xiapu" written on the stele. Hundreds of years later, this may be comparable to the tomb of Su Xiaoxiao. After walking for about two miles, I arrived at a mountain gate. There was a pile of incense ashes, forming a small mound in the forest. It was burned, so from a distance, there was a light cloud of mist. I was speechless. After entering the temple, I visited Yuquan Pond. There were several houses around the pond, built with funds from Cen Chunxuan. Schools of goldfish swam back and forth in the pond. Most of them were black and several feet long. I asked the monks for bread crumbs and threw them into the water. They all kissed the surface, fighting to be the first to disappear in a flash. The words "Fish Cloud Country" were engraved on the wall, and a couplet by Xun Lu was hung on the pillars of the pavilion: "Fish and people share the spring's clarity, hearts share the spring's purity." This spring originates from the West Mountain, flowing underground for dozens of miles, and only appears here in its true form, which is very clear. Behind the courtyard, there is also a Fine Rain Spring. It is named because the spring water is ejected under the surface of the water, splashing like rain. Yuquan Watching Fish, one of the twenty-four scenic spots of West Lake, is also located here. I took a short tour and left. After passing the mountain gate, I looked back at the mountain clouds, which were still thick on the edge of the forest. I returned to Yue Temple, and it was already dusk. Since I had to leave Hangzhou the next day, I still lingered for the scenery of the lake and mountains. I ordered the boatman to slowly swing out of Yudai Bridge, follow the west bank, turn into Su Causeway, Su Causeway and then circle the west of Santan Yingyue (Three Pools Mirroring the Moon), pass the Huxin Pavilion, and return. The boatman seemed quite surprised by my recklessness. I rewarded him with wine money, and he happily wielded the oar and returned. When I arrived at Lakeside Park, there were thousands of lights. I quietly stood by the lake and blew a kiss to this silver West Lake from afar. The evening mountains were silent, the stars and moon were bleak, as if they all had a feeling of regret at parting.

I only got four poems on this trip, which are not very good. I will record them here to end this article: "Hate the delicate sun in autumn, it seems like spring is coming. The boat rides the wind and is full of the lake. Outside the Qianwang Temple, the willows droop. Even if you don't hear the warblers, it's still pleasant." (The Liulang Wenying, the willow waves and singing orioles, one of the ten scenes of West Lake is next to the Qianwang Temple.) "Holding each other slightly drunk in the night hall, the pressing oars and wind are still sadly cool. Are the lights of the wine shop still there on the way home? The moon is like frost on the west side of Broken Bridge." "Forming a bamboo forest beside the mountain, the car stopped at Longhong's second home. I can't forget a dream until now. Buy Hangzhou tea at the fifth watch." "The feelings of youth are like orchids and sandalwood. Seeing the Mid-Autumn Festival moon in a foreign land, the ruined promise of ten years in a white house. The lights around the building fill the cold lake."

Warmth in My Heart (313) 95

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 15: Sighing at Love in All Directions, Enamored of Greenery in the Room

After Long Ziyun and others ordered the dishes, Ling Zhixiang was the first to suggest calling for companions. The hosts naturally had to agree. Fortunately, both of these companions had their own companions. The waiters brought over the name-calling plates, and Lin Fanzi, who had excellent handwriting, picked up a brush soaked in ink and said, "Tell me your names, and I'll write them down." Knowing that Ling Zhixiang had the most companions, he immediately wrote down four or five of them that he knew. Ling Zhixiang said, "That's too many. Three would be enough." Lin Fanzi said, "Calling for companions isn't just for yourself. It's also for others to see. This is a bit of public accountability. You have a lot of resources anyway, so call a few more for us to appreciate." Ling Zhixiang said, "Calling more is okay, but you have to consider the order." Saying that, he took the stack of name-calling tickets from Lin Fanzi and examined them himself, laughing as he said, "There are so many tricks to calling for companions?" Lin Fanzi said, "There are a lot of tricks to calling for companions, especially with these five tickets of his. They have to be sent out in two groups. It's probably a matter of avoiding each other's faces, like Yin and Xing. The two sides can't meet. If they meet, it'll start a sour wind, so he makes them come one before the other. Is that the idea? But usually, just calling for companions wouldn't cause jealousy issues. It must be that the two are close friends, so that's why he does it this way." Ling Zhixiang hurriedly defended, "No, no. If I called them all at once, they would all come at the same time, causing a commotion for a while, and then scatter. It would be meaningless. And they're all little sisters that everyone knows. After they meet, they only talk about what clothes are the most fashionable, what kind of bangs look best, where you bought your shoes, and whether your diamond rings have been re-minted. Questions like that would come up endlessly, leaving the guests out of the loop, as if the two groups were called specifically for them to talk. What's especially annoying is that they act like a group of friends playing charades, stretching out two fingers, three fingers, asking, 'Is he coming?' No one knows what the 'second' or 'third' they're hinting at means. Calling them to come and make a phone call for me, so I specifically separated the order." Lin Fanzi laughed, "What you say sounds reasonable, but in reality, that's not the case. This is your tactic. Don't think I don't know. People say that two heroes can't stand side by side, so in national politics, to put it nicely, it's called unification. Unification means that one is supreme. It's just that two heroes can't stand side by side. If they stand side by side, they're bound to compete. Women are the same. The so-called 'beautiful women refuse to yield' is just that two females can't stand side by side. If they stand side by side, they're bound to compete. This is a kind of instinct. You treat the ladies in your home the same way."
