Automobile News

Special Commentary

Huanhu Avenue Plan 219

— Yan Ye

The vast Taihu Lake between Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces spans 36,000 qing, with 72 peaks appearing and disappearing within, long renowned for its scenic beauty. The National Government has discussed the idea of a Taihu Lake Park. Subsequently, to improve the scenery, the first priority is to build a Huanhu (around the lake) Avenue. Furthermore, the tranquility of Taihu Lake also relies on the convenience of the Huanhu transportation. Once decided, the two provinces were ordered to work together to realize it as soon as possible. Now, the plan is recorded and described below.

After the two provincial governments received the order to design this spring, the Construction Departments of each province actively prepared, formulating a general plan. Separate surveying teams were dispatched to predict the route in order to estimate the cost. After several months of effort, the route was determined and the cost estimated. Then, personnel were sent again to formally determine the route. The Huanhu route is more than 800 li long. Except for the southwest corner of Taihu Lake, from Yixing in Su to Wuxing in Zhe, about 300 li of the Beijing-Hangzhou Road has been completed, and there is no need to build it separately. There are still more than 500 li to be built. Of these 500 li, 400 li are in Jiangsu Province, and only 100 li are in Zhejiang Province. This is because in Jiangsu Province, from Yiwu to the southern border of Wujiang that connects with Zhejiang, no county roads have been built along the lake. Everything needs to be done from scratch, so the project is vast. In Zhejiang Province, the section of the Beijing-Hangzhou Road along the lake reaches more than 200 li, so its project is only about one-quarter of that in Jiangsu. The width of the road is currently set at 30 feet and will be widened as needed in the future. This is the general situation of the project in the two provinces.

The route through Jiangsu Province was carefully considered. Although the Lvxi-Yixing provincial road has not been built, the route had already been determined when Director Wang Qian was in charge of the Construction Department. However, at that time, there was no discussion of the Huanhu Avenue, so the places passed through were not purely along Taihu Lake. Now, in order to facilitate the Huanhu Road, the route has been changed to be closer to Taihu Lake, so that this road can achieve two benefits at once. Starting from Wuxi, it passes through Yuantouzhu, Jingshe Mountain, Wuli Lake, Nanfangquan, Huadafang Village, Xin'an Town, Wangting, and enters Suzhou territory along East Taihu Lake. Then it passes through Guangfu, Mudu, Wuxian City, Pingwang, Zhenze, and reaches Nanxun in Zhejiang. After this, from Nanxun to Wuxing, it belongs to the Zhejiang Province route, which has also been determined early on.

The cost of building the road in Jiangsu Province is estimated to be at least 2 million yuan. The route is long, and there are many small roads crisscrossing between Wuxi and Wujiang. The soil foundation is difficult to fill, and the cost of bridges and culverts is even greater. The provincial treasury is poor and cannot raise funds. Therefore, 1.975 million yuan has been included in the construction bonds issued as the construction cost of this road, and has been submitted to the National Government for approval. The approximately 400,000 yuan required for the more than 100 li in Zhejiang Province is easier to plan.

The recent work progress: The Construction Departments of the two provinces feel that this road is really needed and must be realized as soon as possible. Although the route has been determined before, for the sake of accuracy, they have each sent surveying personnel from the Highway Bureau to re-survey the front line. After everything is ready, the work can be carried out as soon as the funds are allocated without any obstacles.

The Multi-Cylinder Craze in the American Automotive World 220

— Zhi Zheng

Social fashion favors multi-cylinder engines, with some having as many as sixteen. A major change in the automotive manufacturing world.

During the summer of this year, there was a very strange rumor in the automotive world: that the Cadillac Motor Company had decided not to build twelve- and sixteen-cylinder cars this year. After receiving this news, the Automotive Weekly immediately visited the company manager for his opinion on the matter. He smiled and told the reporter, "These words can only be proven by future facts." Counting the days, it has been several months since summer, and Cadillac's multi-cylinder cars are still being built there, and the rumor has finally gone from heated to cold, from cold to silent.

Because of this incident, the Automotive Weekly was reminded of various observations regarding this issue. Why did the society create such a rumor? Undoubtedly, it must have thought that this matter was important. The magazine is very willing to conduct an in-depth study of the number of cylinders issue in the future for the reference of readers.

According to the magazine's opinion, there are two reasons why multi-cylinder cars (referring to those with more than eight cylinders) have not been developed in the past seven years. There are also two reasons why multi-cylinder cars will not only not be discontinued in the future but will also become more important. In the past seven years, most people have regarded high-priced trains as luxury goods, and only a very small number of people have purchased them. Multi-cylinder cars belong to the high-priced category, so their sales will naturally be affected. Second, the machines of the previous multi-cylinder cars had not yet reached the realm of perfection. How did they evolve? For example, when the car started, many noises had to be produced because there were many cylinders. On the one hand, the maintenance cost was surprisingly high. For the sake of cheapness and convenience, people did not bother to buy multi-cylinder cars. These are two conclusions based on facts. Why do we say that multi-cylinder cars will be developed in the near future? There are not many reasons either, only two points. The first point is because people in society welcome eight-cylinder cars and others. According to the change in social psychology, everyone abandons four-cylinder and six-cylinder cars and competes on eight-cylinder and twelve-cylinder cars. Cars are a kind of business, just like ordinary clothes. If you want to make money, the way to win is to cater to social psychology first. Social psychology tends to focus on multi-cylinder cars, especially eight-cylinder cars, so manufacturers have no choice but to follow. The second point is that high-priced cars have made slower progress, so they cannot win without using multiple cylinders. The reason is this: In recent years, almost the entire automotive world has been dominated by low-priced cars. Low-priced cars keep clamoring for improvement. As a result, because of desperate competition, low-priced cars have gradually obtained all the advantages of high-priced cars. In this way, high-priced cars are panicked. In order to maintain their superior position and compete with low-priced cars, they have to find another way. Otherwise, it can be said that they will be completely replaced by low-priced cars. So they thought of the multi-cylinder system. Low-priced cars cannot achieve this, so they focus on working hard on this. At the same time, people in society are tired of sitting in low-priced cars and think of multi-cylinder cars again. In this way, a sudden turning point has occurred in the automotive world again.

Talking about the history of eight-cylinder cars is also very interesting. Eight-cylinder cars were produced in 1915. At that time, there were two companies manufacturing them. The following year, the number suddenly increased to twelve. In 1917, two more companies were added. In 1918, due to business decline and the outbreak of the European War, the number decreased to thirteen. After 1919, it plummeted even further, with only seven or eight remaining. In 1921, it rose to eleven. In 1922, two more were added. In 1923, there was no change. In 1924, it decreased again. The most impressive thing is that in 1928, it jumped from fourteen to nineteen. The following year, it rose to twenty-two, so it had a very rapid upward trend. This year, it has reached the highest number of twenty-seven companies. The founders of the eight-cylinder cars in 1915 are worth mentioning. These are Cadillac and Packard, and during this period, Packard was the first to create twelve-cylinder cars, followed by Cadillac.

Now everyone feels a strong interest in multi-cylinder cars, but we want to ask whether the cost will increase if there are more cylinders. The answer to this question was positive in the past, but it is negative now. Because the current multi-cylinder cars have been improved more than before when they are manufactured. The first thing they pay attention to is the cost problem. Because if this difficulty is not overcome, they cannot compete with low-priced cars. So now we can say that the cost of multi-cylinder cars is not higher than that of any low-priced car. Needless to say, the consumption of car oil, even the repair cost in the future, will not increase because there are more cylinders. Since multi-cylinder cars have these advantages, plus they can generate great power and run quickly, they are welcomed. And twelve-cylinder and sixteen-cylinder cars make people feel excited. However, in our opinion, sixteen cylinders are not needed yet. First, American road laws are very strict and often limit the speed of vehicles. The speed shall not exceed a certain number of miles per hour, so even if there is a car with a great speed, it will ultimately be a hero without a place to use it and cannot take effect. Moreover, if the speed can be fast to a considerable extent, there will be malpractices. For example, the biggest reason for causing accidents is based on the speed problem. Ten years ago, the highest speed of a car was 70 miles per hour, and it was usually only 30 miles. Now, it can travel 100 miles per hour, but only 45 miles are used. So although the car can be fast, it is ultimately difficult to use. Therefore, multi-cylinder cars with sixteen cylinders are probably not needed for the time being except as a fashion.

From the above, we can know that although multi-cylinder cars failed in the past seven years, they have now recovered. Not only have they recovered, but everyone feels a strong interest in them, and there is a tendency of "Multi-Cylinder Craze." The reasons are nothing more than the changes in people's hearts and the internal improvements. The curiosity of Americans is the most obvious in the world. Since this psychological change, the manufacture of multi-cylinder cars must be greatly developed. However, in the opinion of our magazine's reporters, eight cylinders are the most suitable for multi-cylinder cars. Twelve and sixteen cylinders are not very useful. However, car companies cater to the psychology of people in society after all.

When everyone thinks that twelve-cylinder and sixteen-cylinder cars are fashionable, they will naturally produce them as well (Translated from Automotive Weekly).

On the Installment Payment System in the Automotive Industry 221

— Ke Jia

According to statistics from the local East Continental Bank, all old car mortgage loans in the first half of this year have exceeded last year's business volume. It is gratifying to see such progress in this era of economic depression.

Earlier, when local car dealerships first implemented the installment payment system a few years ago, people predicted that it would not have good results. At that time, various experts discussed the benefits of this system and its impact on finance, and there was no consensus. The United States was particularly concerned, because in 1925, the annual sales in the United States had reached US$5,000,000,000.

Opponents of the installment payment system said that the sales of cars, household labor-saving machines, new clothes, radios, and various furniture have opened up new markets and can never meet the needs of the old installment payment system.

Supporters said that large-scale production can increase wages, and high wages mean the ability to make installment payments. Since the installment payment system became popular, the machines for large-scale production have been working non-stop. The above is a continuous cycle, but most critics still do not believe it.

In 1925, the New York Citibank Gazette published opinions against the installment payment system. Others, such as Senator Lames Couzens of Michigan, also strongly criticized it.

But in 1930, the New York Citibank's August Gazette, in view of the fact that the installment payment system had withstood risks and remained as solid as a rock, changed its tone as follows:

It said, "Although we cannot be sure of the final result of this system at present, because the length of the economic depression is closely related to this system, most people predict that the disputes of this system are exaggerated. Also, according to the records of major banks today, all have benefited greatly.

"According to bank reports, the records of all leading car banks in the United States prove that this installment payment system, if implemented properly, will not leave any weakness in the economic system."

The Success Story of the New Buick (2) 222

— Li Jiren

The new Buick straight-eight-cylinder car has been enthusiastically welcomed by all walks of life since it was launched. Today, the wheels of the new Buick are all over the world, and people from all countries have expressed the same enthusiastic welcome, realizing General Motors' slogan: "Only Buick can build beautiful cars."

The foundation of the new Buick's success lies in the beginning. According to Ke Lishi Wa Yun (manager of Shanghai General Motors), the value of orders placed before the new car was manufactured has exceeded US$150 million, which is not an exaggeration. Every year before the new model is launched, old Buick owners have already reserved one to replace it every year and enjoy the taste of a new car. This year's Buick has been greatly improved with eight cylinders, oil temperature limiter, double carbonizer, dual-use intake silencer and air purifier. The simultaneous meshing transmission method is a feature of the transformation in the past three years and is the reason why people in the automotive industry are sincerely welcoming it.

Success lies in excellent construction. The success story of Buick in the past 26 years also lies in this. To date, more than 2.6 million Buick cars have been manufactured, and there are still 1.5 million cars running around the world. According to research, 88% of old Buick owners now purchase new Buick cars, and the annual sales account for half of all types of cars.

The cars manufactured by the Buick factory are not used as test products by car owners, which is also a major reason for their success and an important point for making car owners happy. Buick carefully considers all mechanical improvements or new inventions from a long-term perspective and conducts thorough tests in advance. Therefore, the launch of the new Buick car has three years of field testing and precise research.

Youth Garden

Camping 225

— A-Lu

It was around Wednesday when a white paper with black text and a blue stamp, a children's notice, was posted on the patriotic bulletin board of our school:

[Tonight, the Boy Scouts will hold a camping trip. All members must gather at the large playground at 3:00 PM for inspection...]

Upon receiving this order, the Boy Scouts put on their uniforms in the morning. Before 3:00 PM, the playground was already filled with yellow soldiers. Usually, these girls are elegant and graceful, but today, they transformed into spirited and energetic "Eighth Masters," shouting and jumping, wielding sticks and axes. Their every move was just like soldiers. Who would recognize them as young ladies?

Around 3:00 PM, the loud bell rang more than twenty times. When the Yellow Team leader blew the whistle, the Boy Scouts immediately lined up facing south. At this moment, the large playground was silent except for the wind whistling through the treetops. Mr. Zhang Zhongren, the head of the Boy Scouts, came to inspect, just as soldiers wait for their superior officers. Mr. Zhang, accompanied by Mr. Sun, just walked onto the playground. The awaiting "little soldiers" all raised their sticks in salute.

After the inspection, the Yellow Team leader gave the order to set up camp at the designated campsite. They had to carry all the supplies themselves. It wasn't a problem for those with more strength, but the poor, weaker girls were all panting and out of breath. Although they felt tired, none of them were willing to fall behind. Everyone worked hard. In half an hour, the four large camps were completely set up. Then, some fetched water, some washed vegetables, some cooked rice, and some cooked dishes. Each task was clearly assigned. Even the toilet was prepared by some. When the food was ready, everyone sat on the ground to eat. Although the dishes were not great, they were driven by interest and didn't mind the poor quality of the food. Instead, they found it interesting. Usually, they couldn't finish two bowls, but today they ate three or four. Those who usually ate three or four bowls, needless to say.

The West Garden, which was usually deserted, suddenly became the center of excitement. The Boy Scouts not only occupied this wasteland, but other young ladies also came to join in the fun. One girl, facing the visiting classmates, shouted loudly, "Military camp, no unauthorized personnel allowed!" However, this attracted the attention of some mischievous young ladies. They bravely rushed forward and completely snatched away Xi's hat, food bag, etc. Later, Xi had to apologize to them several times to retrieve the stolen items.

The most interesting thing about camping is raiding the camp, but it is also what they fear the most. Therefore, defensive measures were set up in front and behind the camp. When the camping order was first issued, many people wanted to raid the camp, but seeing their thorough defenses, everyone became fearful. In the end, only two people actually did it.

After twelve o'clock, the young ladies were all tired and one by one crawled into the tents to dream their dreams of fighting on the battlefield and charging to kill the enemy. Who would have thought that someone would come to steal things? Miss Yu, although young, was very brave. In the dark night, she walked alone into their camp to carry out her camp raid. Although Miss Yu was not born a thief, she had a wealth of knowledge about thieves. Before entering their camp, she first made some dog barks and then threw a handful of sand. Seeing that there was no reaction inside, she quietly entered and stole four or five items, returning peacefully.

Miss Yu, who came first, was victorious, but Mr. Sun, who came later, suffered a great loss. Mr. Sun not only lacked Miss Yu's carefulness, but also lacked the common sense of a thief. He wore loud leather shoes and carried a five-hundred-foot flashlight in his hand. Turning on the flashlight wasn't a problem, but his pair of noisy leather shoes had already alerted several people before he even stepped into the camp. They saw the flashlight and knew the camp raider was coming, but they remained silent, waiting for Mr. Sun to enter the camp to steal something. Just as he was about to take an item, the soldiers from the west camp had already surrounded him. When the siren blew, the other three camps all came out. At this time, Mr. Sun was helpless under the light of dozens of flashlights. The Yellow Team leader ordered someone to guard Mr. Sun while inspecting the items. As a result, they found that four items were missing and forced Mr. Sun to return the stolen items. At this time, Mr. Sun shouted that he was wronged, but the soldiers ignored whether he was wronged or not and kept forcing him to return the stolen items. Fortunately, the Yellow Team leader was wise and punished Mr. Sun lightly, letting him go.

Male and Female Students Fighting for Dorms at Labor University 226

— You Wen

The campus of Jiangwan Labor University was originally the model factory. Because of the short construction time and the difficulty in building, the dormitories for both male and female students were modified from the existing factory buildings. There were many shortcomings, and the students naturally did not want to live there for a long time. Especially the female students' dormitory, each room accommodates more than ten people, and the noise is even more inconvenient.

This autumn, a magnificent and exquisite new dormitory was built, but it can only accommodate about one hundred people. The students of the Engineering College and the Social Sciences College began to compete for the ownership of the new building before the new building was completed. A group of female students also secretly lobbied the school authorities early on to allow the

Page 26

half of the east end of the new dormitory downstairs to be used as a residence for female students. The school authorities did not clearly designate or announce this matter. However, the high wall in the middle of the back building indicated that everyone tacitly acknowledged this was the female students' dormitory. Because the allocation and disposal of dormitories were not easy, and the school itself was in trouble, the authorities did not have time to plan this matter. A brand new dormitory, which was the focus of everyone's attention, has been locked down by the "Iron General" until now.

Unexpectedly, the day before yesterday evening, around 9:00 PM, several students from the Engineering College suddenly decided to launch a "house-grabbing" movement. After breaking into the new building, all they saw was people moving boxes, taking quilts, and transporting things, like a scene of terror during a fire. In a short while, all the new rooms were fully occupied by those who were quick. The incident was initiated by the students of the Engineering College, and the students of the Social Sciences College were the ones who suffered. Because they received the news later, it was too late to act, and most of them could only look on with disappointment. However, some unwilling disappointed people, in a fit of anger, ignored everything and invaded the area of ​​the female students downstairs on the east end. They posted name cards on the doors of the rooms, made up the beds, and fell asleep, pretending to be the owners of the new rooms.

Of course, the female students were furious when they heard the news. They really thought this was a barbaric act of trampling on women's rights and despising female students, and they had to rise up to protest. Therefore, the next morning, several brave female students took advantage of the male students' sweet dreams and suddenly broke into the rooms, tore up the name cards on the doors, and moved in their own boxes, baskets, and other items, throwing the male students' things aside, indicating that they were asking the male students to get out. Thus, the dispute over housing arose.

After a long debate, the two sides could not resolve the issue. Both sides' arguments had seemingly reasonable grounds. The female students said, "This is clearly a female dormitory acknowledged by the school authorities. Otherwise, why would they build that wall in the middle? And everyone generally recognizes that male and female students should live separately. What reason is there to mix into our dormitory?" The male students also raised three points to refute, saying, "First, the school authorities did not clearly designate or announce that this was a female dormitory. The wall built in the middle is not necessarily a sign of separation between men and women. Aren't there also partition walls in our male students' old dormitories (the partition wall between the Social Sciences College and the Engineering College)? Second, according to the principle of equal opportunity, in the situation last night, every member of Labor University had the opportunity to grab a new room, and the gains and losses should be attributed to their own skills. Female and male students are both members of Labor University. Third, and moreover, Labor University is a revolutionary school that stands before the times. In the past, there has never been a boundary between male and female students. Working, attending classes, and eating have always been mixed together. Why should living be an exception?"

This kind of debate would of course not have good results. Although later, the more gentle male and female students were willing to withdraw, the main forces of both sides were unwilling to give up. Therefore, a situation of mixed male and female living was successfully created. Some of the more courageous female students, ignoring the male students' encirclement, bravely lived alone or two or three people in a room. It is said that the most commendable among them is the "Da Wu Wei" (Great Fearless) lady. She actually embraced her usual "Da Wu Wei" spirit, went alone (living in a room by herself), deeply surrounded, and resisted effectively, with her spirit always undiminished. This has become the current housing unsolved case of Labor University.

After this incident, it attracted many onlookers from outside the school to visit, some praising and some criticizing. However, the school's guidance class ultimately believed that this was not very convenient, and that over time, it would cause trouble and would not be good for the school's reputation. Therefore, they ordered the male students to voluntarily withdraw, but the male students put forward a condition, which was to order all the students occupying the new dormitory to withdraw together, and then use a lottery method to determine each person's room, and then they would agree to withdraw from the female students' dormitory. However, this matter was very difficult.

With no other choice, the guidance class could only issue a notice acknowledging that the unauthorized move to the new dormitory was invalid. As for the allocation issue, it would be replanned after the new president arrived at the school. However, mixed male and female living is still a fact.

Art World

Random Talks on the German Theater Scene 228

Stepped Stage and Expressionist Director Aisner

Aisner is the stage director of the National Theatre. His stage is the opposite of the soft colors, lyrical poetry, and fairy-tale style stages favored by Reinhardt. He loves to use straight lines and strong colors to express a kind of clear simplicity. He newly created a stage setting for Shakespearean plays, using steps to control the complex scenes unique to Shakespearean plays. Therefore, when people talk about him now, they think of the stepped stage. Recently, he adapted Aitken's [Earth Spirit] into a film. In the third act, he set up many steps as usual.

In the play [Richard III], the dark stage is covered with red steps. The bedroom scene in [Othello] has a white curtain hanging in the center of the dark stage, along with a bed. A white candlestick is placed on the left. This is the bed of the black protagonist in white. This bed is made of four sections of steps. The whole stage can achieve a simple black and white taste, which is a very impressive device. His unique style can achieve a very effect in Shakespeare's military dramas or crowd dramas. The helmets or flags of the soldiers move under the steps. Two or three ancient warriors rise or fall from the steps, which is a very expression of the power of the crowd, which is incomparable to the stupid method of using many disorderly crowds to express it.

The masterpiece that best represents Aisner's set design is the stage surface of Aitken's [Count Fontancreat]. In a room surrounded by white screens, the very thin, straight-legged chairs are all black. The costumes of the characters on stage are also all black. The male protagonist's clothing style has sharp angles on the shoulders and is triangular from the waist down. The female's clothing style is all straight lines. The color is only black and white, except for the hair on the head, which is dazzling gold. The movements of the actors also all take straight-line movements. In a certain scene of this play, you can hear the music of a garden party. This is the musicalization of Expressionist painting, which makes people feel the emotion of seeing the paintings of Expressionist painter Beckmann.

He has always used the name [Young Stage] to put on second performances with the aim of recommending the scripts of unknown writers. The play list is [People Above Demons], and the performance method is completely Expressionist.

The product color of the Expressionist stage is the fragrance of art wandering in the middle. Expressionist drama has been successful, and Aisner's simplicity has also been successful. This is also the reason why Aisner's name and Expressionist drama will be immortal.

The Difficulty of German Theater Scripts

When Halink's [Murder] and Kaiser's [Two Olives] lonely decorated the Expressionist drama scene, it was difficult to find anything more outstanding in the German theater scene for a while. Although there were [Blunner], [Brecht], and [Chaplin]'s author Fischer and [Drunken Boat]'s author Zacchi and sculptor Barlach developing with [Young Stage], they did not give the theater scene anything new. Even the venerable author Waller of [Collective Human Beings], although he was out of prison, only wrote poetry and did not see his activities on the theater scene.

In recent years, foreign scripts have been rampant on the German theater scene. The first to be proud was Pirandello, who led his own troupe to Germany, making the whole of Germany admire his works for a time. His works were often performed in more than ten places. [Honesty is Joy] was performed in thirty-one places. [Man, Animal and Virtue] was performed in fifteen places. The name of [Six Characters in Search of an Author] has become a popular idiom in Germany. The famous theater critic Karl Jakob expressed his difficulty in the lack of German writers and specially wrote an article titled [Six Million People in Search of an Author] to express his feelings. Six million is exactly the total population of Germany.

Following Pirandello was Shaw, and then O'Neill. In addition to these works by English, American, and Italian writers, Chinese plays based on Eastern themes have become popular on the theater scene. [Chulanji] made by Grabent was performed at the [German Theatre] by Reinhardt, and later it was performed in various cities. Reinhardt's interest in Chinese plays is a continuation of his inherent Romanticism, not purely his exotic taste. When he revived Mozart's musical dance drama [The Magic Flute], he took many patterns from Chinese lacquerware on the stage. [Chulanji] is regarded as his second work of Chinese taste. The heroine in this play is Bai Kulei, who became famous for acting Shaw's script. Many places on the stage of this play imitate Japanese Kabuki, such as using bright peach blossoms and red short machines and wide sleeves to express Oriental taste. These are not Chinese but Japanese, and the words [Ogami Lantern] are written on the lanterns on the stage, but they are the lanterns used in Japanese shrines. This is the place where Reinhardt made a mistake.

In addition to [Chulanji]'s Chinese plays, there are also Piercey's [Dong Luo] and the opera [Li Taibai Divine Duck], etc., but none of them are as sad as [Chulanji]. No wonder [Chulanji] is so popular in Germany.

In the midst of such a voice of German writers' lack of success, Crosman, who became famous as a teenager, was expressed. He is the son of the old writer Thomas Mann. When his [Anja and Estelle] was performed in Hamburg, the two heroines were Mamera, the surviving daughter of Aitken, and Eliga, the daughter of Thomas Mann and the sister of the author. The author's acting of the bloodline has become a very interesting thing at the time.

The German theater scene, which was warned by Karl that [Six Million People in Search of an Author], will not always be so lonely (Su).

Japanese Nika Association Bursts 229

— Lin Yong

Tokyo Communication

This is something worthy of our attention

It was during the break time that I also put down my paintbrush. In a very short time, I had to run to the newspaper reading room to find the news that was announced yesterday. Sure enough, a very noteworthy piece of news caught my attention. Indeed, this piece of news is worthy of our attention.

This is the Nika Association, the highest authority of the Japanese field art group. It burst. The Nika Association's burst is a tragic history of the Nika Association, and a little bit of light in the Japanese art world. Because the parts that burst out are all important painters in the Nika Association, and they are the radical vanguards of the Japanese art world.

The Nika Association can compete with the Imperial Art because it is all about the times and the super-era expression, and the strong resistance to the imitation and rules of the enemy. But unfortunately, the Nika Association burst. It burst after the 17th exhibition.

Although the reduction of the Nika Association group's strength is common, the joiners are always stronger than the leavers. Now, the loss is indeed very light. It is difficult to predict whether the joiners in the future will be as strong and brave as the leavers. Perhaps Nika will be weaker from now on. But the Nika Association, which has already obtained more than ten years of old history in the Japanese art world, cannot be easily weakened, I think.

Japanese people like to come up with strange and novel things. However, a group of Nika Associations running in front of the Japanese modern art world, their vanguards ran away, ran out of the scope of the Nika Association, and went to chase their own goals. The vanguard beast group, how sad is this for the Nika Association, which has the power to resist the Imperial Academy of Art? If Nika wants to continue its original glory and strength, unless it continues to work hard and carefully to seek out that hardworking and intelligent writer.

This group of radical writers of the Nika Association, this beast group, they gathered the famous generals of other associations and inserted a [Independent Art Association] on the Japanese art scene. This is because they each already shone like stars in the sky on the Japanese art scene.

If their strength is insufficient and their efforts are not strong and then they fall, then there is no saying that is natural. But the strength of this group is indeed not thin. They are all the main writers of Nika, and they are one-third of the main writers of the Nika Association, and they are all the vanguards of Nika.

The works of this beast group are running to the forefront of Japanese modern society. They are expressions of ridicule, resistance, ugliness, and escape. They are strong impulsive silver.

The initiators of this [Independent Art Association] are Katsuzo Satomi, Yoshizo Kojima, Nika Association members Shigeyoshi Hayashi, Takeshi Hayashi, Takashi Nakayama, Afu Suzuki, Zentaro Kojima, Yasutoku Suzuki, Nika Association member Kawaguchi Kiga, Toji Shimizu, and Ren Ito. They are the winners of this year's Nika Association, saving the rest. One is a non-reviewed member of the Shunyo Association and one is a member of the Diet. The first exhibition will be held on January 10 next year. Wait and see.

Most of them withdrew from the 1930 Art Association and joined the Nika Association last year. This 1930 Art Association was also a very powerful group in Japan. However, since the split last year, since the death of a pillar, Kiyokawa Zenji, this year, it has sunk to seeming to be destroyed. Therefore, in this prosperous period of the Nika Association, this group has withdrawn again. This Nika Association in the future is very worthy of our attention, and the Imperial Academy of Art has suddenly collided with a powerful field group, which is also the same worthy of our attention.

I wrote this completely as a report, a report to my dear art teachers and friends.

Now the teachers in the school have told me that they are very alarmed and sighing, and even outsiders are generally very surprised.

Art World Contribution Guidelines 230

(1) The text should be about the latest art (painting, music, sculpture, architecture, drama, etc.) and literary news, reviews, and introductions at home and abroad.

(2) Photos should be limited to recent portraits and works of domestic and foreign writers, and various photographs related to the words.

(4) The number of words per article should not exceed 2,000 at most.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the paper.

(6) Do not write horizontally. Do not write in a sloppy manner. Western text can be omitted. If it is unavoidable to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.
